My actual experience began before I entered her office.  When I was quoted $900 for an extraction.  In fact my former dentist had quoted me about 2/3 of the price Dr Vakili charged me for half of the work.
From my very first phone call with the adorable Jessie, and the way he raved of her service, I immediately felt I was speaking to a trusted friend.
That is the warmth and kindness I have received from every member of the office.
Hannah was my hygienist, and I could go on and on about her excitement and joy. She is sincerely interested in me and my teeth even taking extra time to help me find a quality toothbrush on line.
Zuzu does the billing and she can stretch a dime like it's made out of rubber.  I cannot say this enough.  The price you are quoted is the price you pay NO MATTER WHAT.  No little fees or tricks to confuse you after the fact. Additionally she is nice and works with your insurance to do the most.
Aya did my fittings and was sweet and quiet.  Everything she did fit perfectly.  Her work is impeccable.
Finally, I was fortunate to have both Dr Vakili and well as the talented Dr Leila do an extensive surgery on me.  It included multiple extractions and implants, as well as surgically raising my sinus cavity.  It took about 4 hours.  Fewer than 24 hours later, I am cleaning my house and feeling great.  My pain is completely controlled by Advil.  These results are so incredible, if it were not for the stitches  I wouldn't think they did anything at all.
And as a final side note, I refused any and all opiates.  Dr Vakili was extremely aware of the epidemic and welcomed the opportunity to work around that.  I was sedated completely and absolutely comfortable without the use of opiates.
What more can I say? Go to Solana Smiles.  Don't wait.  Go now.</review>

<Rating>5< /Rating></record></dataset><record>
<review>Must have the chicken and waffles! Nice comfortable spot. Could be considered a hidden gem. Being a classically trainded Chef myself for over 12 years and working for the upper 3% of society I definitely think Green Street Cafe is a good spot. My girlfriend had the french toast. The french toast was good not rubbery and came out hot which is always a plus. I on the other hand order the chicken and waffles and let me tell you WOW! was I impressed. The chicken was soft, tender, juicy and well seasoned and the cheddar bacon waffle was delicate and crisp with delicious undertones of bacon, vanilla and cheddar. (Comes with jalapenos in the waffle as well but I opted that out) The sausage gravy that comes atop the chicken and waffles was excellent as well. It was rich, creamy, balanced and alround good. YUM, GREAT JOB GSC! I must admit though this was my first experience there and have yet to try more items on the menu but be assured I will be returning with high hopes :)

Side notes to GSC.
Dora the server was excellent, great service and energy. With such a great dish available to your customers maybe consider having 100% maple syrup as an option or just adding it to your breakfast items.
I brought my own today as I do any time I go out looking for good breakfast spots and let me tell you it really makes all the difference. Coffee was moderate at best. We had two cups and the were both lacking in body and flavor. Just a recommendation maybe try Pete's or Kirkland signature Organic.< /review><pics>None</pics>< Rating>
5<//Rating>

< Review>
Popped in for Sunday brunch for a table for 3. The wait was about 30 min, which wasn't terrible given the rush.

We sat outside on the covered patio and ordered immediately. I ordered the breakfast burrito and the coffee - because I noticed a sign that said Lavazza coffee...SOLD!!

The service was friendly, but I could tell it seemed like everyone was running around given how busy they were. The food was good and fresh, but nothing that blew my mind away from the dish that wanted me to scarf it down other than being hangry.

Overall, great place for local food. There is plenty of parking in the shopping strip. I would also suggest to buffer about 20 min of wait time given how busy they are.</Review>

< Review>
Can't say enough great things about Dave and the entire crew at Grizzly. We started working with them about two years ago (when our winery moved into a new location) and the experience could not have been better. Dave came out for an estimate, we talked through a few different options and he put together a super-competitive quote (one that even included some of my thoughts). When it came time for install...Dave and John were there on time and even managed to finish the job ahead of schedule. It is worth noting that we had several different trades in the building at the same time...but that didn't seem to bother them at all. After things were wrapped up, Dave took the time to program each component of the system and go over all the specifics (it's kind of a complicated set-up...at least for a novice like me).

And their service after the fact is spot on as well. We've had to call them out a couple of times for issues (equipment defects) and they have always come through...usually within an hour or two. For our money...Dave and the folks at Grizzly are just the best.<//Review>

< review>
I really like this place; the menu exactly hits the spot for anyone looking for a great lunch spot with modest prices and has a variety of flavor palettes.

In one meal I had an Italian item and an Asian item; both were executed flavorfully (not bland) and thoughtfully (the flavors were exciting and authentic).

Not only that, but there are many different platforms for the flavors, whether by bowl, bun, wrap, or noodle.

Importantly, the portion sizes were satisfying!

Finally customer service and speed is good. I don't know if it's their preferred method, but if you're not able to call, they also take orders by email. Useful for detailed orders or during a work meeting!<//review>

I found this nice little hidden gem/ golden nugget of a place very close to my work location and their menu items are phenomenal!! They open at 7:30am every weekday and they have an awesome selection of food items to choose from: Omelettes, bagels, sandwiches, burgers, wraps, bowls, salads, soups, teriyaki chicken or beef plates, fried rice plates, smoothies and even includes healthy food options, and/or vegetarian options. < Review>
Hands down the best food in Ontario. I used to work in the area from 2014 to 2016 tried everything around here. The wait can be long during the busy lunch hour, but it is worth waiting for (or taking your lunch a little later to avoid the crowd). I came back to try it out today (August 2018) and everything was just as good as I remembered. Same friendly owner and same great food. I'm definitely coming back here next time I'm in town.</Review>

<Time>1506721512003<//Time><Rating>5< /Rating>< review>
I have been unable to eat bread for years and thought I was allergic to wheat. A lady sitting next to me in a Hollister restaurant  recommended I try this bakery as they use only organic products and mill their own flour.  Sure enough, I have had none of the cramping, bloating etc. that I normally experienced when I ate other breads. Having said that, their bread or pastries and all of their products are delicious. Additionally  they are super nice to deal with. We called in our order a day ahead of time and it was ready when we arrived. Hours of operation are quite limited (Friday afternoons and Saturday's until 3) but they have maintained the quality and therefore it made our 200 mile (round trip)  drive worth it .</review>

<Review>Funky little place off of Divis where all sorts of people hang out - the crowd had some older couples, college kids, etc. It gets really crowded on a weekend night as the evening goes on and I believe there's a cover after 9 PM. <Rating>3< /Rating>< review>
Pretty crowded on a Thursday night, and found that people were a bit more hesitant to dance than the music invited (maybe it was just the night/time I was there).

I like the space a lot, and a pretty large bar in the back. The music was super fun dancing music, too.

The location is awesome, right on the Wiggle (if you're by bike) or Divis (if you're in the city).

I would definitely check it out again, it's always pretty busy and have seen big linds on the weekend (rightfully so -  michael jackson night!)</review>
